name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:10 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:During the May Day holiday, I brought my child to the Jiangsu Garden Expo Park in Nanjing. My child likes amusement parks, so I chose the Westin closest to the Bobo Park.
The location of the Westin is really good. It is a 10-minute walk from the Bobo Park, or one stop away from the sightseeing bus line 2. It is very convenient. The hotel called a few days before check-in and gave me the electronic ticket for the Garden Expo Park, and the entrance was very smooth.
It was around 3:30 in the afternoon when I checked in. There were many people because of holidays, but it was quite fast. I was given a wristband for the sightseeing bus, as well as a handmade class coupon and a small train ticket in the set meal. The layout of the hotel is a bit strange. The room is located relatively inside, and it takes a long time to walk in every time. The room is not bad, quite clean, with a balcony, and the children like it very much.
During the stay, I only ate at the all-day restaurant. Breakfast and dinner were good. The staff's service was warm and thoughtful. The dishes were not many but quite exquisite. There were a lot of people for breakfast. The hotel arranged a banquet hall as the breakfast area, so it was very fast to be seated. It is worth mentioning that during dinner, a chef was arranged to take the children to experience making donuts. The children had a lot of fun and the adults had a comfortable meal, which was highly praised.
The children's favorite is undoubtedly the swimming pool and hot springs. Westin has two pools, one large and one small, with a suitable temperature and a lot of fun. The children's club is indeed large and more suitable for relatively small children.
The only complaint is that the sound insulation is really not very good. We are used to sleeping late, but we were woken up by the talking in the corridor very early, which was a bit depressing. Overall, the Garden Expo Park is still very suitable for walking children, and Westin is also a good choice.

The hotel itself is located in the picturesque Garden Expo Park Scenic Area. The Garden Expo Park currently implements different hotels to enter from different entrances. Westin is currently the No. 4 gate Jinxiu Gate, which can be entered by entering the park by SMS. Westin's concierge staff were very attentive. They informed me of these details by calling and texting the day before. As long as they follow their introduction and guidance, it will be fine. The hotel is deep in the park. It is recommended to drive by yourself or let an online car-hailing driver deliver it to the inside. Do not get off at the entrance of the Garden Expo.
The exterior of the hotel is a cool and calm brown fa√ßade. The overall style reminds me of the cabins in Switzerland during a ski vacation. There is no towering and towering hotel that is often seen in downtown hotels. Although the volume is large, the design is light. I agree with a relaxed and happy state of mind. One side of the hotel is facing the Garden Expo Park Scenic Area, passing through the foyer, and the other side of the hotel is the large floor-to-ceiling windows in the lobby, which is the best viewing point to enjoy the Jingyang Building in the scenic spot. Standing in the lobby bar and outdoor terrace at night, the Jingyang Building is bright with neon lights and immortals. Gong Haomiao is reminiscent of the prosperous years of "a thousand lights in the night market illuminate the blue clouds".

For hotels, especially resort and relaxation hotels, Tianzhimeng beds are always trustworthy, and a lot of local Nanjing cultural elements are incorporated into the decoration, such as blue and white porcelain wall decorations imitating plum blossoms. Because the hotel rooms are newly opened, the overall maintenance is nothing to say, clean and tidy. If there is a slight deficiency, I think there are two points that need to be improved. The first is that there should always be a meal delivery menu in the guest room. At present, the menu will be delivered to the guests immediately after the customer service is on the phone. The service is very timely and thoughtful, but after soaking in the hot spring When you go to the hotel, you are often hungry, and waiting for an extra second is a kind of torment; the second is that the hotel's current TV projection system is slightly insufficient, you can only choose mobile phone or tablet projection, and it must be limited to a few apps, Not being able to choose others freely, and not being able to choose a laptop, makes me feel a little sorry that I want to watch a movie before going to bed at night.
The hotel has good food and beverages, especially the buffet breakfast, which is rich in variety. Personally, I must highly praise westin's breakfast duck blood vermicelli soup. Guests can freely add duck offal ingredients. As a duck heart and duck gizzard fanatic, I can't love it more. The day we checked out coincided with Laba, and the hotel also provided Laba porridge, which added a little taste of the New Year. Near the hotel are Yangzhou Garden and Lianyungang Garden. They also have their own restaurants. If you like, you can also walk or drive there. The hotel concierge and front desk staff will be very enthusiastic to provide maps and guides.
The first floor of the hotel is currently a hot spring, a gym and a spa. The overall environment is also very good, especially the gym environment is quite satisfactory. My mother no longer has to worry that I will gain weight if I can't keep my mouth shut during the vacation.
After staying at the Westin Hot Spring Resort Hotel in the Garden Expo Park, it was really the busiest time of the year before, and I never had a moment to rest. I hope that the blood that the hotel has given me will allow me to survive this period of years ago! ! ! !
